Capital Market Authority roles, regulations and contacts

12 Jul 2024, 00:00

How well do you know the agencies in your country? Come to think of it, not so many people can tell what some government agencies and regulatory bodies do. One such body whose role remains unknown to many Kenyans is the Capital Market Authority (CMA). CMA is an independent public agency entrenched in Cap 485 A of the constitution and is established by an Act of parliament. It is an arm of the National Treasury and Planning and is meant to supervise, license and monitor capital market activities.

New Year's Eve - Facts, Info, Trivia

08 Mar 2024, 00:00

Annual festivity celebrated across the world with varying traditions. The holiday celebrates the final day of the year according to the Gregorian calendar, which is the predominantly observed calendar across the world.  Trivia In the U.S., the most well-known celebration is on Times Square in New York City, where a mechanical ball slowly drops during the last minute of December 31. There are multiple TV specials that cover the ball drop, including Dick Clark's New Year's Rockin' Eve, which was hosted by Dick Clark almost every year from 1973 to 2012.

What Happened to Miep Gies and Her Husband Jan?

24 Feb 2024, 00:00

What happened to Miep Gies and her husband? They helped Anne Frank's family go into hiding during WWII, and Miep saved Anne's diary.
